Treewait2      = '<' / 'b'

Treerecv       = '^' / 'd'
Treebuild      = '.' / 'h'
Treeupdate     = '~' / 'm'
Treehmaxupdate = '|' / 'n'
Treemisc =       ':' / 'r'
Domain decomp  = '+' / 'l'
Density compute= '"' / 'o'
Density imbal  = '/' / 'p'
Density commu  = '`' / 's'
Density misc   = ',' / 'f'
Hydro compute  = '>' / 'i'
Hydro imbalance= '@' / 'g'

Hydro misc     = '&' / 'e'
